<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Paolo_Monti_-_Servizio_fotografico_(Bolzano,_1957)_-_BEIC_6356404.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1280" data-file-width="1010" decoding="async" height="279" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Paolo_Monti_-_Servizio_fotografico_%28Bolzano%2C_1957%29_-_BEIC_6356404.jpg/220px-Paolo_Monti_-_Servizio_fotografico_%28Bolzano%2C_1957%29_-_BEIC_6356404.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Paolo_Monti_-_Servizio_fotografico_%28Bolzano%2C_1957%29_-_BEIC_6356404.jpg/330px-Paolo_Monti_-_Servizio_fotografico_%28Bolzano%2C_1957%29_-_BEIC_6356404.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Paolo_Monti_-_Servizio_fotografico_%28Bolzano%2C_1957%29_-_BEIC_6356404.jpg/440px-Paolo_Monti_-_Servizio_fotografico_%28Bolzano%2C_1957%29_-_BEIC_6356404.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Paolo_Monti_-_Servizio_fotografico_(Bolzano,_1957)_-_BEIC_6356404.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Installment by L. Gargantini for the Bolzano fair, 1957. Photo by <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Monti" title="Paolo Monti">Paolo Monti</a> (Fondo Paolo Monti, <a href="/wiki/Biblioteca_europea_di_informazione_e_cultura" title="Biblioteca europea di informazione e cultura">BEIC</a>).</div></div></div>
<ul><li>EN 527 Office furniture – Work tables and desks</li>
<li>EN 1335 Office furniture – Office work chair</li>
<li>ANSI/BIFMA X 5.1 Office Seating</li>
<li>DIN 4551 Office furniture; revolving office <a href="/wiki/Chair" title="Chair">chair</a> with adjustable back with or without arm rests, adjustable in height</li>
<li>EN 581 Outdoor furniture – Seating and tables for camping, domestic and contract use</li>
<li>EN 1728:2014 Furniture – Seating – Test methods for the determination of strength and durability– updated in 2014.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77"><a href="#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup></li>
<li>EN 1730:2012 Furniture – Test methods for the determination of stability, strength and durability.</li>
<li>BS 4875 Furniture. Strength and stability of furniture. Methods for determination of stability of non-domestic storage furniture (<a href="/wiki/British_Standards" title="British Standards">British Standard</a>)</li>
<li>EN 747 Furniture – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bunk_beds" title="Bunk beds">Bunk beds</a> and high beds – Test methods for the determination of stability, strength and durability</li>
<li>EN 13150 Workbenches for laboratories – Safety requirements and test methods</li>
<li>EN 1729 Educational furniture, chairs and tables for educational institutions<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup></li>
<li>RAL-GZ 430 Furniture standard from Germany</li>
<li>NEN 1812 Furniture standard from the Netherlands</li>
<li>GB 28007-2011 Children's furniture – General technical requirements for children's furniture designed and manufactured for children between 3 and 14 years old</li>
<li>BS 5852: 2006 Methods of test for assessment of the ignitability of upholstered seating by smouldering and flaming ignition sources</li>
<li>BS 7176: Specification for resistance to ignition of upholstered furniture for non-domestic seating by testing composites</li></ul>

<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1097025294">.mw-parser-output .side-box{margin:4px 0;box-sizing:border-box;border:1px solid #aaa;font-size:88%;line-height:1.25em;background-color:#f9f9f9}.mw-parser-output .side-box-abovebelow,.mw-parser-output .side-box-text{padding:0.25em 0.9em}.mw-parser-output .side-box-image{padding:2px 0 2px 0.9em;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .side-box-imageright{padding:2px 0.9em 2px 0;text-align:center}@media(min-width:500px){.mw-parser-output .side-box-flex{display:flex;align-items:center}.mw-parser-output .side-box-text{flex:1}}@media(min-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .side-box{width:238px}.mw-parser-output .side-box-right{clear:right;float:right;margin-left:1em}.mw-parser-output .side-box-left{margin-right:1em}}</style><div class="side-box side-box-right plainlinks sistersitebox">
<div class="side-box-flex">
<div class="side-box-image"><img alt="" class="noviewer" data-file-height="355" data-file-width="300" decoding="async" height="40" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Wikiquote-logo.svg/34px-Wikiquote-logo.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Wikiquote-logo.svg/51px-Wikiquote-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Wikiquote-logo.svg/68px-Wikiquote-logo.svg.png 2x" width="34"/></div>
<div class="side-box-text plainlist">Wikiquote has quotations related to <i><b><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikiquote.org/wiki/Special:Search/Furniture" title="q:Special:Search/Furniture">Furniture</a></b></i>.</div></div>

<div class="side-box-image"><img alt="" class="noviewer" data-file-height="1376" data-file-width="1024" decoding="async" height="40" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/30px-Commons-logo.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/45px-Commons-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/59px-Commons-logo.svg.png 2x" width="30"/></div>
<div class="side-box-text plainlist">Wikimedia Commons has media related to <span style="font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;"><a class="extiw" href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:Furniture" title="commons:Category:Furniture">Furniture</a></span>.</div></div>

<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.maltwood.uvic.ca/hoft/timeline.html" rel="nofollow">History of Furniture Timeline</a> <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20200114064922/http://www.maltwood.uvic.ca/hoft/timeline.html" rel="nofollow">Archived</a> 14 January 2020 at the <a href="/wiki/Wayback_Machine" title="Wayback Machine">Wayback Machine</a> From Maltwood Art Museum and Gallery, University of Victoria</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/files/12254/12254-h/12254-h.htm" rel="nofollow">Illustrated History Of Furniture</a></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://hearth.library.cornell.edu/" rel="nofollow">Home Economics Archive: Tradition, Research, History (HEARTH)</a> <br/>An e-book collection of over 1,000 books on home economics spanning 1850 to 1950, created by Cornell University's <a class="external text" href="http://www.mannlib.cornell.edu/" rel="nofollow">Mann Library</a>. Includes several hundred works on furniture and interior design in this period, itemized in a <a class="external text" href="http://hearth.library.cornell.edu/h/hearth/bibs/applied.pdf" rel="nofollow">specific bibliography</a>.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://libmma.contentdm.oclc.org/cdm/search/collection/p15324coll10/searchterm/American%20furniture%20in%20the%20Metropolitan%20Museum%20of%20Art/field/title/mode/exact/conn/and/order/nosort" rel="nofollow"><i>American Furniture in The Metropolitan Museum of Art</i></a>, a fully digitized 2 volume exhibition catalog</li></ul>
